1. F-P谐振腔的实际应用是什么，工作原理是什么？ - 知乎

  • 链接：https://www.zhihu.com/question/56707047
  • 来源：bing
  • 摘要：F-P谐振腔是法布里-珀罗（Fabry-Pérot）谐振腔的简称，它是由两个平行的反射镜构成的光学谐振腔。 F-P谐振腔在光学和激光领域有着广泛的应用，用于光学干涉、激光器、传感器、光谱学等方面。 工作 …
  • 易漏细节梳理：

F-P谐振腔由两个平行的反射镜构成，这种设计使得它在光学和激光领域中具有广泛的应用。首先，F-P谐振腔能够用于光学干涉，通过调节两个反射镜之间的距离，可以精确控制光的干涉效果。其次，它在激光器中也发挥着重要作用，通过调节谐振腔的长度，可以有效控制激光的波长和稳定性。此外，F-P谐振腔还被应用于传感器领域，通过检测谐振腔长度的变化，可以实现对微小变化的敏感检测。因此，F-P谐振腔不仅在光学干涉和激光器中具有重要应用，还在光谱学和传感器技术中展现出其独特的价值。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • F-P谐振腔由两个平行的反射镜构成。
  • F-P谐振腔广泛应用于光学和激光领域。
  • F-P谐振腔可用于光学干涉。
  • F-P谐振腔可用于激光器。
  • F-P谐振腔可用于传感器。
  • F-P谐振腔可用于光谱学。

2. 电压谐振的电流谐振的区别有哪些？ - 知乎

  • 链接：https://www.zhihu.com/question/619580057
  • 来源：bing
  • 摘要：2023年8月28日 · 在电阻、电容、电感串联电路中，出现电源、电压、电流同相位现象，叫做串联谐振，其特点是：电路呈纯电阻性，电源、电压和电流同相位，电抗X等于0，阻抗Z等于电阻R，此时电 …
  • 易漏细节梳理：

在串联谐振状态下，电路表现出特定的特性。首先，当电路达到串联谐振时，电抗X会降至0，这意味着电感和电容的相互作用完全抵消，只有电阻R对电流产生影响。其次，阻抗Z在串联谐振时等于电阻R，表明此时电路的总阻抗仅由电阻决定，没有额外的电抗分量。此外，由于电抗X为0，串联谐振时电源、电压和电流同相位，即电压和电流的相位差为0，这使得能量在电路中以最小的损耗进行传输。因此，串联谐振不仅简化了电路分析，还提高了能量传输效率。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 串联谐振时电抗X等于0；
  • 串联谐振时阻抗Z等于电阻R；
  • 串联谐振时电源、电压和电流同相位。

3. 品质因数Q如何理解？ - 知乎

  • 链接：https://www.zhihu.com/question/635207276
  • 来源：bing
  • 摘要：2023年12月16日 · LC谐振回路的品质因数Q，本质是：谐振回路谐振时，一个振荡周期内，谐振回路内储存的能量与损耗掉的能量之比。 为了使得 Q 与角频率 \omega 容易对应起来，可将两个能量之比乘 …
  • 易漏细节梳理：

品质因数Q是衡量LC谐振回路性能的重要指标，它反映了回路中能量存储与损耗的比例关系。具体而言，品质因数Q值越高，表明回路中能量的损耗越小，能量存储的比例越大，回路的谐振特性就越明显。因此，对于需要高效能量存储和传输的应用场景，提高LC谐振回路的品质因数Q显得尤为重要。品质因数Q不仅影响着回路的谐振频率稳定性，还决定了回路的选择性，即能够更有效地滤除非谐振频率下的信号。因此，优化设计以提升Q值，是提升LC谐振回路性能的关键步骤。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 品质因数Q反映了LC谐振回路中能量存储与损耗的比例。

4. 量子到底是什么？是粒子？还是一种理论？ - 知乎

  • 链接：https://www.zhihu.com/question/597611446
  • 来源：bing
  • 摘要：量子力学：微观世界的本质 后来我们发现， 微观世界的物理量在大多数情况下都是量子化的，连续变化的才是少数。 很多科学家对量子力学做出了重要的贡献，如普朗克、爱因斯坦、德布罗意、玻尔、 …
  • 易漏细节梳理：

量子化的物理量在大多数情况下是不连续变化的，这一特性在量子力学中尤为显著。相比之下，连续变化的物理量在量子力学中则属于少数情况。量子力学不仅是一个理论框架，它还精确地描述了微观世界的实际现象。因此，量子化不仅影响了物理量的变化方式，还深刻地改变了我们对物质世界的理解，使其更加符合量子力学的原理。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 量子化的物理量在大多数情况下是不连续变化的。
  • 连续变化的物理量在量子力学中是少数情况。
  • 量子力学不仅是理论，还描述了微观世界的实际现象。

  • 易漏细节梳理：

科学家们对观测为何会导致量子态坍缩的具体机制尚未完全明了，这使得这一过程显得神秘莫测。然而，与公众普遍认为的相比，科学家们实际上对量子力学的原理有着更为深入的理解。尽管如此，"裸量子力学"理论并未完全解决观测导致坍缩的问题，这表明在量子力学的解释上仍存在未解之谜。因此，尽管科学家们对量子力学的理解已经相当深入，但在观测导致坍缩的具体机制上仍需进一步探索和研究。

  • 科学家们比一般人想象的更清楚量子力学的原理。
  • "裸量子力学"并未完全解释观测导致坍缩的问题。

6. 如何系统性讲清楚量子、质子、光子、光量子、夸克、离子 ...

  • 链接：https://www.zhihu.com/question/400339390
  • 来源：bing
  • 摘要：2021年3月8日 · 题主问题中的几个小问题： 1、光子即光量子。人类研究光的本质时经历了 粒子说---波动说---粒子说---波粒二象性说。光量子一词最早由爱因斯坦提出。光子静质量为0，光子的动质量（能 …
  • 易漏细节梳理：

粒子说认为光是粒子，波动说则认为光是波动，这两种观点看似矛盾，实则共同揭示了光的本质。光量子和光子是同一概念，指的是光的量子化单位，这一概念最早由爱因斯坦提出，用以解释光电效应。光子的静质量为0，但具有动质量，这使得光子能够表现出波动性和粒子性，即波粒二象性。这种特性不仅挑战了传统的物理学观念，也为量子力学的发展奠定了基础。因此，光量子和光子不仅是理解光本质的关键，也是探索量子世界的重要工具。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 粒子说认为光是粒子，波动说认为光是波动。
  • 光量子和光子是同一概念，指光的量子化单位。
  • 爱因斯坦最早提出光量子的概念。
  • 光子的静质量为0，但具有动质量。
  • 光子展示了波粒二象性。

晶体管的工作原理基于量子力学效应，其核心在于通过控制电子的量子态来实现信息的放大和开关。布洛赫的工作为这一理论提供了坚实的数学基础，他的研究成果为晶体管的发明奠定了重要的理论基础。晶体管因此成为量子力学在现代科技中应用的一个重要实例，不仅极大地推动了电子设备的发展，还深刻地改变了信息时代的面貌。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 晶体管的工作原理基于量子力学效应。
  • 布洛赫的工作为晶体管的发明奠定了理论基础。
  • 晶体管是量子力学在现代科技中的重要应用实例。

8. 光子是量子吗，电子是量子吗？ - 知乎

  • 链接：https://www.zhihu.com/question/420323704
  • 来源：bing
  • 摘要：2020年9月9日 · 光子盒研究院出品 前言：基础研究是科技创新的基石。鉴于此，光子盒增设“量子前沿”全新栏目，旨在介绍量子科技的一系列基础技术、相关进展及现状前景。 我们对量子信息的兴趣出现 …
  • 易漏细节梳理：

量子信息的基础在于量子力学中的基本粒子，如光子和电子。光子作为量子力学中的基本粒子，其行为遵循量子力学的规律，而非经典物理学的规律。同样，电子也具备量子力学的基本粒子特性。这些量子粒子的量子性质使得它们在量子计算和量子通信中扮演重要角色。然而，由于这些量子性质容易被忽略，它们对量子技术的重要性往往被低估。光子和电子的量子性质是量子技术发展的基石，因此，量子信息科学强调对这些量子粒子的量子性质的利用和研究，以推动量子技术的进步。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 量子信息的基础是量子力学中的基本粒子，如光子和电子。
  • 光子是量子力学中的基本粒子。
  • 电子也是量子力学中的基本粒子。
  • 量子信息的研究基于对量子粒子的精确理解和操控。
  • 光子和电子的行为遵循量子力学的规律，而非经典物理学的规律。
  • 光子和电子的量子性质使得它们在量子计算和量子通信中扮演重要角色。
  • 量子粒子的量子性质容易被忽略，但对量子技术至关重要。
  • 光子和电子的量子性质是量子技术发展的基石。
  • 量子信息科学强调对量子粒子的量子性质的利用和研究。

  • 量子通信利用了量子纠缠的特性。
  • 量子密钥分发和量子密码通信是重要应用。
  • 传统加密方式可能无法抵御量子通信的攻击。

10. 能否通俗地解释一下，什么是量子纠缠？ - 知乎

  • 链接：https://www.zhihu.com/question/20322494
  • 来源：bing
  • 摘要：2015年1月12日 · 能否解释得通俗一些，最好能举一些例子。 据我所知，有两种观点。 一是爱因斯坦认为 量子纠缠 只不过是这样，一双手套，分别装入保险箱，一个送往北极，一个送给你，当你打开箱 …
  • 易漏细节梳理：

量子纠缠是一种奇特的量子现象，其中两个粒子即使相隔很远，一个粒子的状态变化会瞬间引起另一个粒子状态的变化。爱因斯坦曾将量子纠缠比喻为一双手套分别放入两个保险箱中，但这种比喻容易让人误解量子纠缠的非局域性。实际上，量子纠缠并不意味着两个粒子之间有某种超光速的通信渠道，它只能用来传递量子态的信息，而不能用来直接传递经典信息。因此，量子纠缠展示了量子力学的非局域性，但并不支持超光速的信息传递。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 量子纠缠中的两个粒子即使相隔很远，一个粒子的状态变化会瞬间引起另一个粒子状态的变化。
  • 爱因斯坦将量子纠缠比喻为一双手套分别放入两个保险箱中，但这种比喻容易让人误解量子纠缠的非局域性。
  • 量子纠缠不能用来传递信息，只能用来传递量子态的信息。
  • 量子纠缠并不意味着两个粒子之间有某种超光速的通信渠道。

  • 易漏细节梳理：

一级数字孪生仅提供物理精确的3D数字表达，这意味着它能够准确地反映物理对象的外观和尺寸，但并不包含任何行为或功能模拟。数字孪生的级别差异反映了其复杂性和功能范围，较低级别的数字孪生仅具备物理精确性，而高级别的数字孪生则能够模拟更多的行为和功能，从而提供更全面的模型。因此，不同级别的数字孪生适用于不同的应用场景，一级数字孪生因其物理精确性而在某些领域具有独特价值。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 一级数字孪生仅提供物理精确的3D数字表达。
  • 数字孪生的表达不包含行为或功能模拟。
  • 数字孪生的级别差异反映了其复杂性和功能范围。

20. 怎么区分概率论中不相关与独立？ - 知乎

  • 链接：https://www.zhihu.com/question/636411935
  • 来源：bing
  • 摘要：2023年12月30日 · 概率论中描述两个随机变量 X 和 Y 之间关系的"不相关"（uncorrelated）和"独立"（independent）是两个重要且不同的概念，这里简单分开介绍一下什么叫做"不相关"以及"独 …
  • 易漏细节梳理：

不相关并不意味着独立，不相关的随机变量可能不是独立的，而独立的随机变量则一定不相关。不相关是指两个随机变量的协方差为零，意味着它们之间没有线性关系，但并不意味着它们之间没有其他形式的关系。因此，不相关不等同于没有关系。相比之下，独立是一个更强的概念，它意味着两个随机变量的取值互不影响，即一个变量的取值不会对另一个变量的取值产生任何影响。因此，独立是比不相关更强的概念。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 不相关并不意味着独立；不相关的随机变量可能不是独立的；独立的随机变量一定不相关；不相关是指两个随机变量的协方差为零；独立是指两个随机变量的取值互不影响；不相关不等同于没有关系；独立是比不相关更强的概念。

22. 如何理解概率论中的独立同分布？请分别解释独立、同分布及 ...

  • 链接：https://www.zhihu.com/question/21418108
  • 来源：bing
  • 摘要：2017年11月1日 · 什么是独立同分布 指随机变量A，和另一个随机变量之间是否是独立同分布 说白了，就是比较两个或多个随机变量之间： ① 其中一个随机变量可能的取值是否会受其他变量 …
  • 易漏细节梳理：

独立意味着两个随机变量的取值互不影响，而同分布则表示两个随机变量具有相同的概率分布。独立同分布要求两个随机变量既独立又具有相同的概率分布，这是对随机变量的一种严格要求。然而，该定义不适用于多个随机变量的情况，需逐一比较每对变量。值得注意的是，常见误解之一是认为独立同分布意味着所有随机变量共享同一参数，实际上，每个随机变量可能具有不同的参数，只要它们之间满足独立同分布的条件即可。因此，理解独立同分布的概念时，应明确其严格的数学定义及其与实际应用中的常见误解之间的区别。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 独立意味着两个随机变量的取值互不影响。
  • 同分布意味着两个随机变量具有相同的概率分布。
  • 独立同分布要求两个随机变量既独立又具有相同的概率分布。
  • 该定义不适用于多个随机变量的情况，需逐一比较每对变量。
  • 常见误解是认为独立同分布意味着所有随机变量共享同一参数。
正文（点击展开）

23. 如何理解编程语言中「流」（stream）的概念？ - 知乎

  • 链接：https://www.zhihu.com/question/27996269
  • 来源：bing
  • 摘要：容器可以被视为一个流，或者可以用流的方式来读写，但流不是容器。 譬如说，网络流（NetworkStream）就不是一个容器，也正因为流不是一个容器，所以流不存在拷贝。 我们可以拷贝 …
  • 易漏细节梳理：

流不是容器，而是描述物质运动状态的概念，它强调的是物质在空间和时间上的动态变化，而非静态的存储。因此，流不存在拷贝，这意味着无法通过复制的方式保存流的状态，因为流的本质是不断变化的，任何试图复制流的行为都会导致信息的丢失或不准确。这种特性使得流在处理动态数据时具有独特的优势，但也带来了对数据处理方式的特殊要求，即必须实时处理流中的数据，而不能依赖于预先存储的数据副本。因此，理解和应用流的概念对于处理实时数据流、网络流量分析以及数据处理系统的设计至关重要。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 流不是容器；流不存在拷贝。

24. 如何形象的理解计算机中“流”的概念？ - 知乎

  • 链接：https://www.zhihu.com/question/38075755
  • 来源：bing
  • 摘要：2018年10月23日 · 你这个流究竟是说Stream还是说Flow啊，这两个意思是不同的，后一个在“网络流”当中用，是完全另一个概念。 Stream的话，在计算机里就是顺序读取或者写入的字节序列。这是很多现 …
  • 易漏细节梳理：

Stream在计算机中指的是顺序读取或写入的字节序列，强调的是字节的顺序处理，而非数据的即时传输。相比之下，网络流中的“流”指的是完全不同的概念。计算机中的“流”与网络中的“流”在概念上存在显著差异，前者关注的是数据的顺序处理，而后者则涉及数据的即时传输。因此，理解这两者之间的区别对于正确处理计算机中的数据流至关重要。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • Stream在计算机中指的是顺序读取或写入的字节序列。
  • 网络流中的“流”指的是完全不同的概念。
  • 计算机中的“流”强调的是字节的顺序处理，而非数据的即时传输。

26. 为何在数学里 Manifold 会被翻译成“流形”？

  • 链接：https://www.zhihu.com/question/44366618
  • 来源：bing
  • 摘要：中文-流形 20 世纪初，我国部分学者与民间团体开始着手科学名词的引入与翻译工作。1919年科学名词审查会成立， 1923 年开始审查数学名词，每次通过审查后的数学名词陆续发表在《科学》杂志上，一 …
  • 易漏细节梳理：

科学名词的翻译工作始于20世纪初，这一过程对于促进科学知识的传播至关重要。1931年，成立了科学名词审查会，其主要职责是对科学术语进行标准化和审查。随后，从1932年开始，审查会专注于数学名词的审查工作，力求确保数学术语的准确性和一致性。审查通过的数学名词被陆续发表在《科学》杂志上，为学术界提供了权威的数学术语标准，促进了数学领域的交流与理解。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 科学名词的翻译工作始于20世纪初。
  • 年成立了科学名词审查会。
  • 年开始审查数学名词。
  • 审查通过的数学名词发表在《科学》杂志上。

28. 什么是串流（Streaming）？ - 知乎

  • 链接：https://www.zhihu.com/question/359315470
  • 来源：bing
  • 摘要：2021年7月10日 · 在网速能超过USB读写速度的今天，低画质根本不需要压缩就能直接实时传输，这算不算串流，就要问专业人士了。 再来实际举例，哪些情况使用了串流技术：通过新浪直播观看世界杯 …
  • 易漏细节梳理：

串流技术允许数据在传输过程中被处理和播放，而无需完全下载，这一特性使得用户能够即时观看视频或听音乐，极大地提升了用户体验。首先，这种技术能够有效减少等待时间，因为用户可以在数据传输过程中开始播放内容，无需等待整个文件下载完毕。其次，串流技术还支持动态调整播放质量，根据网络状况自动调整视频或音频的分辨率和比特率，确保流畅的观看体验。此外，这种技术还能够实现内容的快速更新和版本控制，使得最新的内容可以迅速提供给用户。因此，串流技术不仅提升了用户体验，还增强了内容的灵活性和适应性，成为现代数字媒体传输不可或缺的一部分。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 串流技术允许数据在传输过程中被处理和播放，而无需完全下载。

29. 什么是相量测量单元 (PMU)？ - 知乎

  • 链接：https://www.zhihu.com/question/527652381
  • 来源：bing
  • 摘要：2022年4月13日 · 什么是PMU装置？PMU装置在电网中的作用是什么？ 答：PMU意为同步相量测量装置，即用于同步相量的测量、输出以及动态记录的装置。PMU的核心特征包括基于标准时钟信号的同步 …
  • 易漏细节梳理：

PMU（Phasor Measurement Unit）的核心在于实现时间同步，基于标准时钟信号进行同步，从而能够准确测量和输出同步相量。这种时间同步机制使得PMU能够进行动态记录，确保在电力系统中各相量之间的时序关系准确无误。因此，尽管PMU的某些功能可能容易被忽略，但其在电力系统监控和故障诊断中的重要性不容忽视。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • PMU基于标准时钟信号进行同步。
  • PMU装置用于测量和输出同步相量。
  • PMU能够进行动态记录。
  • PMU的核心在于实现时间同步。

30. 自动化测试 | PMU与PMU有什么区别吗？ - 知乎

  • 链接：https://www.zhihu.com/question/594851077
  • 来源：bing
  • 摘要：在自动化测试中，PMU和PMI是两个不同的概念，它们分别代表着“性能监测单元”和“性能监测接口”。 PMU（Performance Monitoring Unit）指的是一种硬件模块或者芯片，通常用于CPU、GPU等设备 …
  • 易漏细节梳理：

PMU是硬件模块或芯片，而非软件接口，这意味着它负责收集和处理硬件层面的性能数据。与之相对，PMI指的是“性能监测接口”，这是一个与PMU不同的概念，它实际上是一个软件接口，用于提供访问PMU收集的性能数据的方式。因此，PMU和PMI在功能上有所区分，前者是硬件组件，后者则是用于数据访问的软件接口。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • PMU是硬件模块或芯片，而非软件接口。
  • PMU与PMI是两个不同的概念。
  • PMI指的是“性能监测接口”，而非硬件模块。

  • 易漏细节梳理：

量子化现象不仅限于能量，还包括角动量、自旋、电荷等物理量，这表明量子力学是理解和描述微观物理世界的理论基础。量子力学的应用之一是量子密钥分发技术，它能够实现数学上证明的安全经典通信，从而保障信息安全。然而，量子态隐形传输在经典通信中是无法实现的，这进一步突显了量子通信的独特性和优越性。量子通信实验通常以光子为量子态载体，而量子信息的编码空间主要以光偏振为主，这为量子通信的实际操作提供了明确的方向和依据。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 量子化现象不仅限于能量，还包括角动量、自旋、电荷等物理量。
  • 量子力学是理解和描述微观物理世界的理论。
  • 量子密钥分发技术可以实现数学上证明的安全经典通信。
  • 量子态隐形传输在经典通信中是无法实现的。
  • 量子通信实验通常以光子为量子态载体。
  • 量子信息的编码空间主要以光偏振为主。

量子 - 知乎 量子 量子（quantum）是现代物理的重要概念。最早是由德国物理学家M·普朗克在1900年提出的。他假设黑体辐射中的辐射能量是不连续的，只能取能量基本单位的整数倍，从而很好地解释了黑体辐射的实验现象。… 查看全部内容 关注话题 ​ 管理 ​ 分享 ​ 百科 讨论 精华 等待回答 详细内容 简介 量子（quantum）是现代物理的重要概念。最早是由德国物理学家M·普朗克在1900年提出的。他假设黑体辐射中的辐射能量是不连续的，只能取能量基本单位的整数倍，从而很好地解释了黑体辐射的实验现象。 [1] 后来的研究表明，不但能量表现出这种不连续的分离化性质，其他物理量诸如角动量、自旋、电荷等也都表现出这种不连续的量子化现象。这同以牛顿力学为代表的经典物理有根本的区别。量子化现象主要表现在微观物理世界。描写微观物理世界的物理理论是量子力学。量子一词来自拉丁语quantus，意为“有多少”，代表“相当数量的某物质”。自从普朗克提出量子这一概念以来，经爱因斯坦、玻尔、德布罗意、海森伯、薛定谔、狄拉克、玻恩等人的完善，在20世纪的前半期，初步建立了完整的量子力学理论。绝大多数物理学家将量子力学视为理解和描述自然的基本理论。 [2] 量子通信 量子通信的基本思想主要由Bennett 等于20 世纪80 年代和90 年代起相继提出, 主要包括量子密钥分发(quantum key distribution, QKD) 和量子态隐形传输(quantum teleportation)。 量子密钥分发可以建立安全的通信密码, 通过一次一密的加密方式可以实现点对点方式的安全经典通信. 这里的安全性是在数学上已经获得严格证明的安全性, 这是经典通信迄今为止做不到的. 现有的量子密钥分发技术可以实现百公里量级的量子密钥分发， 辅以光开关等技术, 还可以实现量子密钥分发网络。 量子态隐形传输是基于量子纠缠态的分发与量子联合测量, 实现量子态(量子信息) 的空间转移而又不移动量子态的物理载体, 这如同将密封信件内容从一个信封内转移到另一个信封内而又不移动任何信息载体自身. 这在经典通信中是无法想象的事. 基于量子态隐形传输技术和量子存储技术的量子中继器可以实现任意远距离的量子密钥分发及网络。 量子通信的实现基于量子态传输. 为便于传输, 现有的量子通信实验一般以光子为量子态载体, 其表现形式即为光子态传输. 量子信息的编码空间以光偏振为主。 浏览量 2.9 亿 讨论量 16.6 万

DeepSeek官网 - 深度求索DeepSeek网页版在线使用 在线体验DeepSeek满血高速网页版 DeepSeek官网入口网页版 腾讯元宝DeepSeek版 强大的推理能力 DeepSeek 在推理任务上表现出色，尤其是数学、逻辑推理和编程任务。其 R1 模型通过强化学习技术，能够像人类一样进行多步骤的推理和思考，甚至在复杂问题上展现出超越其他模型的能力。例如，在 AIME 2024 数学基准测试中，DeepSeek R1 的得分率达到了 79.8%，与 OpenAI 的 o1 模型相当。 高效的混合专家架构 DeepSeek 采用了混合专家（MoE）架构，这种架构通过动态激活部分专家，大幅减少了计算量，同时保持了高性能。例如，DeepSeek-V3 拥有 6710 亿参数，但每次输入仅激活 370 亿参数，显著降低了计算成本。这种架构不仅提高了模型的效率，还使其能够更好地处理复杂的多任务场景。 创新的训练技术 DeepSeek 在训练过程中采用了多种创新技术，如多头潜在注意力（MLA）机制、多令牌预测（MTP）技术等。MLA 机制通过低秩键值联合压缩，减少了缓存容量和计算复杂度；MTP 技术则允许模型同时预测多个连续位置的 token，提高了训练效率并更好地捕捉 token 间的依赖关系。 开源与低成本 DeepSeek 的开源策略使其在行业内独树一帜。其模型不仅完全开源，还提供了详细的训练代码和数据，方便开发者进行定制和优化。此外，DeepSeek 的训练成本也远低于其他同类模型。例如，DeepSeek-V3 的训练成本仅为 557.6 万美元，而 OpenAI 的类似模型训练成本则高达数亿美元。 广泛的应用场景 DeepSeek 的应用场景非常广泛，涵盖了智能对话、文本生成、代码辅助、数学推理、文件解析等多个领域。无论是学生、研究人员还是企业用户，都能从 DeepSeek 中受益。例如，DeepSeek-Coder 能够帮助开发者快速生成代码、修复漏洞，DeepSeek-Math 则可以为学生提供详细的数学解题指导。 灵活的部署选项 DeepSeek 提供了多种部署选项，以满足不同用户的需求。从轻量化的移动设备到高性能的服务器，用户可以根据自己的硬件资源选择合适的模型版本。此外，DeepSeek 还支持私有化部署和定制微调，企业用户可以根据自己的业务需求进行优化和集成。 DeepSeek网页版零门槛使用 无需下载安装或复杂配置，用户只需进入DeepSeek官网即可立即免费使用DeepSeek网页版。这种即开即用的特性让每个人都能轻松体验先进的AI技术，无论是学生、开发者还是企业用户，都能快速上手，享受高效的AI服务。 全功能集成 deepseek网页版完整集成了DeepSeek模型的所有核心功能，包括智能对话、代码生成、文档解析、多语言翻译等。用户可以在统一的界面中完成多样化的AI任务，无需切换不同工具，大幅提升工作效率和创作体验。 持续技术迭代 使用deepseek网页版，用户无需手动更新即可体验到最新版本的AI模型和功能增强。网页版自动同步官方最新技术成果，无论是新模型发布还是性能优化，deepseek网页版都能第一时间为用户提供服务，确保始终处于技术前沿。

  • 易漏细节梳理：

云游戏通过将计算任务转移到服务器端，解决了高配置需求和存储空间紧张的问题，从而降低了玩家的硬件要求和本地存储占用。由于服务器端的算力消耗主要集中在计算任务上，云游戏的帧率通常较低，以降低计算成本，但其画质通常较好。尽管云游戏的帧率较低，但其计费价格通常比本地版本便宜，因此可以提高性价比。此外，云游戏的便捷性得以提高，玩家可以轻松尝试新游戏，避免因新版本更新而等待下载的情况，从而减少了存储空间占用。因此，云游戏不仅提高了游戏的便捷性和可访问性，还通过优化资源分配，降低了玩家的总体成本。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 云游戏版本的本地存储占用非常小。
  • 云游戏可以解决高配置需求和存储空间紧张的问题。
  • 云游戏的计费价格通常比本地版本便宜。
  • 云游戏的帧率通常较低，以降低计算成本。
  • 云游戏的画质通常较好，但帧率较低。
  • 云游戏的算力消耗主要在服务器端。

正文（抓取，非 AI）

云星铁已经开测，继云原神后米家又要增添一位「云」成员了。 说起来，米家游戏上云版也快变成一种共同趋势了，若论原因，核心关键词当然还是为了一个 「方便」 —— 无需下载体积庞大的客户端或是更新包，真正做到随开随玩，并且可以让玩家无视设备配置享受超高清画质游戏。 这毫无疑问是一项有力的推广优势。 同时，通过与业界新秀蔚领时代展开的深度合作，米在云游戏方面拥有了成熟技术支持与运维经验，作为让蔚领赚到第一桶金的项目，隔壁云原神已经积累了相当数量的用户，成为一部分玩家的首选体验方案。这点由云原神可以单独登上 APP 付费榜也能看得出来， 说明了「云」玩家的需求可一点不小众。 云版 APP 都能单独上畅销榜单，这说明有相当数量的玩家选择通过云通道体验游戏 有优势，又有成功先例，星铁考虑上云游戏自然也就成了顺水推舟之事。 从玩家视角来看，云星铁也的确会带来一些好处。这就不得不吐槽一下了，星铁的配置需求其实真要比最开始想象中要高一些（捂脸），手机玩长了还是会变暖宝宝，耗电量也比较大。 同样，在存储空间消耗方面星铁也称不上「迷你」。到目前的 1.5 版本，游戏安卓客户端已有 13 G 之大，PC 端也已达到 25 G，可以预见随着未来开拓之旅抵达更多星球，游戏体积会越来越大（当然了，这是游戏为了保证品质与内容量所产生的必然需求），这点对设备存储空间有些紧张的朋友确实会比较头疼 —— 既不想忍痛割爱卸载游戏，又苦于需要更多空间存储其他资料。 云版游戏本地存储占用永远只有可以忽略不计的几百兆 云游戏就能很好地解决以上这两项困扰，实际上，相当一些玩家在移动端选择云原神体验游戏正是基于这个原因。 话说回来，隔壁原神已经借助云游戏技术「降级」为网页游戏了，等云星铁正式推出，变「网页小游戏」岂不也是指日可待？别的不说，这样就能很好解决 Macbook 玩家游玩的需求了（以及利好摸鱼党……懂的都懂，咳）。 由于采用了相同的支持平台，所以云星铁与云原神基本是一个模子，但也存在一定区别。比如大家应该比较最关心的计费方面， 云星铁的目前官宣的计费价格只有云原神的一半 ，无论是畅玩卡（云星铁月卡 30 元 vs 云原神月卡 60 元）还是云玩币（云星铁 1 元/小时 vs 云原神 2 元/小时）均是如此（每日领取免费游戏时长这点是一样的）。 其实光靠领免费时长都足够满足不少朋友的日常体验了，某种意义上来说星铁真的完美适配云游戏 另外，同云原神最高 60 帧相比，云星铁将画面帧率上限限制在了 30 帧。 不过这块的限制也完全可以理解，毕竟较便宜的价格摆在那里。星铁作为一款回合制箱庭 RPG，在游玩时本身就不需要⾼频率、高时效性的操作，而且大多时候游戏行为就是打开右上角自动按钮挂机刷本（自动木人桩：别忘了还有我！），玩家多数时候是不会盯着看的。所以限定 30 帧其实算是一件比较无所谓的事，你帧数高也不可以多打一回合（雾）。 大部分时候其实都在开自动挂机 （相较之下，在身为 ARPG +开放世界游戏的姐姐原神那边，玩家对帧数的敏感性就高得多了，一方面战斗中需要进行高频率实时操作，获取及时反馈是一种刚需，特别是挑战 BOSS 和打深渊时，另一方面探索广袤的开放世界时为了获得更舒适的体验也需求更高的帧率。） 对云游戏技术有一定了解的朋友大概知道，任何游戏性能指标的提升放在云游戏服务领域中都等价于对算力消耗的加剧， 越高的帧率 & 越好的画质，就意味着云服务的计算成本越⾼。 目前云游戏是把游戏包拿回来放到云上计算，有一万的玩家玩就有一万客户端在云上计算，从经济学角度来看边际成本是固定的，等于每增加一个玩家就增加一个客户端，这套结构本身搭建成本就比较高，同时还很难优化。 相比本地客户端游戏，云游戏的算力消耗几乎全在服务器端，所以有句话叫「云游戏的本质是计算价值的转移」，而服务器端部署以及运维产生的一系列固定成本是减不下来的，不优化就容易陷入云成本困境 这波等于是制作组依据星铁自身的特点，经过市场调查和研究后为云游戏版本选择了一条「成本领先」的道路，在游戏体验基本没受多少影响的前提下，设法节约了比较弹性的计算成本，并将之转化为玩家侧更高的性价比，个人认为这是一套能称得上双赢的正确策略。 当然云星铁目前也还处在测试阶段，如果这块呼声较高，相信制作组那边应该也会考虑提上优化日程的（他们回应反馈一直都很迅速），大家不妨实际体验后根据自身感受进行反馈。 总的来看，推出云星铁能够比较有效地提升游戏便捷性，打破对硬件设备条件的依赖，进一步降低玩家尝试新游戏的门槛来促进扩圈，同时较低的付费标准还具有价格优势。 对于打算长期游玩游戏的玩家而言，云服务版游戏也提供了不少方便之处，至少就我个人而言，等云星铁出来我就可以和原神一样卸载手机上的普通客户端了，这样一下又少了个十几 G 大的巨无霸 APP，而且……再也不会发生新版本更新后发现自己忘了更新游戏，在那苦等下载更新包的情况了（笑），岂不美哉？

V3最新版本DeepSeek-V3-0324在代码生成、数学推理、对话交互等方面全面进阶！代码能力得分328.3，超越普通版Claude 3.7 Sonnet（322.3分）。支持大白话描述需求，秒出可用代码（如动态天气网页卡片）。新增"省流模式"，日常问答响应速度更快。对话更自然，会主动反问需求，插入表情符号调节气氛。访问官网或App，体验更智能、更流畅的AI交互！ 技术架构：6850亿开源模型，推理大幅提升 DeepSeek采用混合专家（MoE）架构，6850亿参数模型免费开源（MIT协议），推理时仅激活约370亿参数，降低硬件需求。支持128K长上下文，超长对话更稳定。新增"多头潜在注意力（MLA）"和"多Token预测（MTP）"技术。可在消费级硬件（如M3 Ultra Mac）高效运行。API支持JSON输出，max_tokens上限提升至64K。 未来展望：更强大的R2和多模态AI即将到来 DeepSeek的研发蓝图更是令人期待。即将推出的 R2 模型，预计参数规模将达到 1.2 万亿，采用自研 Hybrid MoE 3.0 架构，动态激活参数达 1.2 万亿，这将使其性能实现质的飞跃。同时，团队正在全力研发多模态支持功能，不久后，用户将能够与模型进行图像、音频交互，比如通过描述画面生成对应图像，进一步拓展 AI 应用边界，赋能更多领域。 DeepSeek网页版是基于官网接口开发的跨平台AI应用，无需下载安装即可随时访问使用。作为新一代智能创作工具，它完美适配DeepSeek电脑版、手机版和小程序多终端，提供7×24小时不间断的智能服务体验。平台内置强大的AI对话系统，能够精准理解用户需求，无论是工作难题还是学习疑问都能获得专业解答；创新的AI绘画功能可将文字描述转化为多种风格的视觉艺术作品；智能视频制作工具从脚本生成到剪辑输出一站式完成；AI音乐创作让零基础用户也能轻松谱写专属旋律；高效的PPT生成功能帮助用户快速制作专业演示文稿。   • 易漏细节梳理：

首先，DeepSeek 网页版可能比官方版本更快速稳定，而其 R1 满血版的性能与 OpenAI 的 o1、o3相当，但成本更低。DeepSeek 的应用范围广泛，涵盖智能对话、AI搜索、文件处理等多个领域。尽管 DeepSeek 官网可能繁忙，但建议使用平替网站以获得更好的访问体验。DeepSeek R1-32B 模型拥有 320 亿参数，可在 24GB 显存显卡上流畅运行，而 R1-8B 模型则有 80 亿参数，适用于 8GB 显存显卡。此外，DeepSeek-V3 支持 128K 长上下文处理，生成速度提升至 60 TPS，且在数学竞赛中超越了闭源模型如 GPT-4。DeepSeek-V2.5 是 V2 系列的升级版本，于 2024 年 9 月发布，DeepSeek-V3 在数学竞赛中表现出色。DeepSeek-R1-32B 和 R1-8B 模型分别适用于不同显存需求的用户。DeepSeek-VL2 是视觉语言模型的升级版，多模态理解能力更强，而 DeepSeekMath 专注于数学推理，DeepSeek-Prover 用于定理证明。Janus-Pro-7B 是基于视觉的模型，于 2025 年 1 月 27 日推出，进一步丰富了 DeepSeek 的应用生态。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • DeepSeek 网页版可能比官方版本更快速稳定。

  • DeepSeek 的应用范围广泛，包括智能对话、AI搜索、文件处理等。
  • DeepSeek 官网可能繁忙，建议使用平替网站。
  • DeepSeek R1-32B 模型可以在 24GB 显存显卡上流畅运行。
  • DeepSeek-R1-8B 模型适用于 8GB 显存显卡。
  • DeepSeek-V3 支持 128K 长上下文处理，生成速度提升至 60 TPS。
  • DeepSeek-V2.5 是 V2 系列的升级版本，发布于 2024 年 9 月。

47. Approximating Entanglement Based on Abstract Interpretation

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.10056v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Entanglement is a fundamental property of quantum systems, essential for non-trivial quantum programs. Identifying when qubits become entangled is critical for circuit optimization, and for arguing for the correctness of quantum algorithms. This paper presents a static analysis method for approximating entanglement by extending an already existing abstract interpretation, thus avoiding the exponential slowdown of an exact analysis. The approach is shown to be sound and an implementation is provided in Standard ML with linear-time scalability.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

entanglement 是量子系统的基本属性，对于非平凡的量子程序至关重要。然而，准确分析纠缠会导致指数级的性能下降，因此静态分析方法被提出，用于近似纠缠并避免精确分析的指数级减速。这种静态分析方法不仅适用于量子算法正确性的论证，还具有线性时间的可扩展性，使得其实现更为高效。此外，entanglement 的识别对于电路优化至关重要，因此在量子计算中，识别和管理纠缠成为了一个关键步骤。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • entanglement 是量子系统的基本属性，对于非平凡的量子程序至关重要。
  • 准确分析纠缠会导致指数级的性能下降。
  • 静态分析方法可以近似纠缠，避免了精确分析的指数级减速。
  • 该方法适用于量子算法正确性的论证。
  • 实现该方法的代码具有线性时间的可扩展性。
  • entanglement 的识别对于电路优化至关重要。

48. ProjectNeura/MIPCandy: A Candy for Medical Image Processing

  • 链接：https://github.com/ProjectNeura/MIPCandy
  • 来源：bing
  • 摘要：MIP Candy is Project Neura's next-generation infrastructure framework for medical image processing. It integrates a handful number of common network architectures with their corresponding training, …
  • 易漏细节梳理：

MIP Candy 提供了一个灵活且可扩展的框架，便于医疗图像处理研究者快速原型设计。它只需覆盖一个方法即可创建适用于你网络架构的训练器，从而大大简化了开发流程。MIP Candy 还支持 Notion、WandB 和 TensorBoard 等前端平台，确保了实验数据的可视化和管理。此外，它提供了无缝支持自定义实验的大量易于使用的技术，使得研究者能够轻松调整和优化实验设置。MIP Candy 还具备恢复中断实验的功能，确保研究过程的连续性。更重要的是，MIP Candy 内置了 2D 和 3D 可视化工具，便于直观理解实验结果，而其构建完整的实验管道仅需 10 秒，极大地提高了研究效率。需要注意的是，MIP Candy 需要 Python >= 3.12 的环境支持。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • MIP Candy 提供了灵活且可扩展的框架，便于医疗图像处理研究者快速原型设计。
  • MIP Candy 只需覆盖一个方法即可创建适用于你网络架构的训练器。
  • MIP Candy 支持 Notion、WandB 和 TensorBoard 等前端平台。
  • MIP Candy 提供了无缝支持自定义实验的大量易于使用的技术。
  • MIP Candy 可以恢复中断的实验。
  • MIP Candy 提供了内置的 2D 和 3D 可视化，便于直观理解。
  • MIP Candy 需要 Python >= 3.12。
  • MIP Candy 可以在 10 秒内构建完整的实验管道。

Additionally, it also provides integrations with popular frontend dashboards such as Notion, WandB, and TensorBoard. We provide a flexible and extensible framework for medical image processing researchers to quickly prototype their ideas. MIP Candy takes care of all the rest, so you can focus on only the key experiment designs. 🔗 Home 🔗 Docs Key Features Why MIP Candy? 🤔 Easy adaptation to fit your needs We provide tons of easy-to-use techniques for training that seamlessly support your customized experiments. Sliding window ROI inspection ROI cropping to align dataset shape (100% or 33% foreground) Automatic padding ... You only need to override one method to create a trainer for your network architecture. Satisfying command-line UI design Built-in 2D and 3D visualization for intuitive understanding High availability with interruption tolerance Interrupted experiments can be resumed with ease. Support of various frontend platforms for remote monitoring MIP Candy Supports Notion , WandB, and TensorBoard. Citation Should you find our work helpful to you, please cite our publication. Installation Note that MIP Candy requires Python >= 3.12 . Quick Start Below is a simple example of a nnU-Net style training. The batch size is set to 1 due to the varying shape of the dataset, although you can use a ROIDataset to align the shapes. 49. Modeling financial transactions via random walks on temporal networks

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.20713v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：We model financial transactions as random walks on activity-driven temporal networks. By enforcing fund conservation, our framework analytically derives heavy-tailed distributions for the stationary balances and transaction sizes. Crucially, the latter is driven by variance in the spending propensity of individuals. Calibrated with empirical data from a closed, digital currency community, the model also reproduces observed correlations between inflows and outflows. Our findings provide a path for understanding emergent properties of the circulation of money.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

随机游走模型被用来模拟金融交易，这导致了余额和交易规模的重尾分布。交易规模的波动性差异进一步影响了交易规模。模型通过使用一个封闭的数字货币社区的实证数据进行校准，能够再现流入和流出之间的相关性，并确保资金的保守使用。通过这种方式，模型能够探索货币流通的涌现特性。为了更准确地模拟这种动态，活动驱动的时间网络被用于建模。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • random walks model financial transactions;
  • heavy-tailed distributions arise for balances and transaction sizes;
  • spending propensity variance drives transaction sizes;
  • model is calibrated with empirical data from a closed digital currency community;
  • observed correlations between inflows and outflows are reproduced;
  • fund conservation is enforced in the model;
  • emergent properties of money circulation are explored;
  • activity-driven temporal networks are used for modeling.

50. Error Accumulation using Linearized Models for Aggregating Flexibility in Distribution Systems

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.04382v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：This paper investigates flexibility aggregation approaches based on linear models. We begin by examining the theoretical foundations of linear AC power flow, two variants of so-called DC power flow, and the LinDistFlow model, along with their underlying assumptions. The discussion covers key system details, including network topology, voltage constraints, and line losses. Simulations are conducted on the KIT Campus Nord network with real demand and solar data. Results show that, in the absence of negative losses, line losses are generally underestimated by linear models. Furthermore, line losses errors tend to accumulate both at the point of common coupling (PCC) and over extended time horizons.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

易漏但重要的线损在电力系统仿真中往往被低估，这主要是由于线性模型对系统细节的假设过于简化。线性模型通常基于线性AC功率流动，而这种模型本身存在一定的假设，比如网络拓扑和电压约束等关键细节。这些假设可能导致在电力系统连接点（PCC）处的线损误差累积，尤其是在长时间运行的情况下。因此，线损对于准确的仿真至关重要，而线性模型的这些假设会导致线损误差的累积，特别是在长时间运行和复杂网络拓扑的情况下。因此，为了提高仿真精度，需要考虑更复杂的模型，如DC功率流动变体和LinDistFlow模型，这些模型能够更好地反映实际系统的复杂性。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • line losses are generally underestimated by linear models
  • line losses errors tend to accumulate at the PCC
  • line losses errors tend to accumulate over extended time horizons
  • linear models make assumptions about system details
  • linear AC power flow has underlying assumptions
  • DC power flow variants have underlying assumptions
  • LinDistFlow model has underlying assumptions
  • network topology is a key system detail
  • voltage constraints are key system details
  • line losses are important for accurate simulations

51. The Iconicity of the Generated Image

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.16473v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：How humans interpret and produce images is influenced by the images we have been exposed to. Similarly, visual generative AI models are exposed to many training images and learn to generate new images based on this. Given the importance of iconic images in human visual communication, as they are widely seen, reproduced, and used as inspiration, we may expect that they may similarly have a proportionally large influence within the generative AI process. In this work we explore this question through a three-part analysis, involving data attribution, semantic similarity analysis, and a user-study. Our findings indicate that iconic images do not have an obvious influence on the generative process, and that for many icons it is challenging to reproduce an image which resembles it closely. This highlights an important difference in how humans and visual generative AI models draw on and learn from prior visual communication.

52. Reducing the Gate Count with Efficient Trotter-Suzuki Schemes

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.21145v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Hamiltonian formulations of lattice field theories provide access to real-time dynamics, but their simulation is difficult to implement efficiently. Trotter-Suzuki decompositions are at the center of time evolution computation, either on quantum hardware or classically, for instance with the use of tensor networks. While low-order Trotterizations remain the standard choice due to their simplicity, higher-order schemes offer the potential for improved efficiency. In this work we outline a short guide to Trotter-Suzuki schemes and their implementations in general. To help with this, we highlight new efficient schemes found by our optimization framework, and demonstrate their performance on the Heisenberg model.

53. Generating twisted Cherednik eigenfunctions

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.21120v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Hamiltonians ${\cal H}^{a}k$ of new integrable systems associated with the integer rays $(1,a)$ (commutative subalgebras) of Ding-Iohara-Miki (DIM) algebra in the $N$-body representation are closely related to commuting twisted Cherednik Hamiltonians $\mathfrak{C}_i^{(a)}$, ${\cal H}^{a}_k = \sum^N (\mathfrak{C}_i^{(a)})^k$. Moreover, symmetric combinations of eigenfunctions in the twisted Cherednik system were recently shown to produce the DIM Hamiltonian eigenstates. We explicitly construct these twisted Cherednik eigenfunctions recurrently by action of some (creation and permutation) operations. It resembles of a far-going generalization of Kirillov-Noumi operators, but exact relation remains to be specified.

55. Nord-Parl-TTS: Finnish and Swedish TTS Dataset from Parliament Speech

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.17988v2
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Text-to-speech (TTS) development is limited by scarcity of high-quality, publicly available speech data for most languages outside a few high-resource languages. We present Nord-Parl-TTS, an open TTS dataset for Finnish and Swedish based on speech found in the wild. Using recordings of Nordic parliamentary proceedings, we extract 900 hours of Finnish and 5090 hours of Swedish speech suitable for TTS training. The dataset is built using an adapted version of the Emilia data processing pipeline and includes unified evaluation sets to support model development and benchmarking. By offering open, large-scale data for Finnish and Swedish, Nord-Parl-TTS narrows the resource gap in TTS between high- and lower-resourced languages.

56. LUTstructions: Self-loading FPGA-based Reconfigurable Instructions

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.20802v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：General-purpose processors feature a limited number of instructions based on an instruction set. They can be numerous, such as with vector extensions that include hundreds or thousands of instructions, but this comes at a cost; they are often unable to express arbitrary tasks efficiently. This paper explores the concept of having reconfigurable instructions by incorporating reconfigurable areas in a softcore. It follows a relatively-recently proposed computer architecture concept for seamlessly loading instruction implementation-carrying bitstreams from main memory. The resulting softcore is entirely evaluated on an FPGA, essentially having an FPGA-on-an-FPGA for the instruction implementations, with no notable operating frequency overhead. This is achieved with a custom FPGA architecture called LUTstruction, which is tailored towards low-latency for custom instructions and wide reconfiguration, as well as a soft implementation for the purposes of architectural exploration.
正文（点击展开）

正文（抓取，非 AI）

57. Anomalous diffusion properties of stochastic transport by heavy-tailed jump processes

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.21097v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：In this work, we investigate the large-scale transport properties of a passive scalar advected by a turbulent fluid, modelled as a superposition of divergence-free vector fields, each weighted by an independent symmetric $α$-stable-like process. Motivated by recent works showing that complex small-scale spatial structures often lead to Brownian dispersion, we study if this principle persists when the driving noise exhibits heavy-tailed jump statistics. Our numerical results show a clear dichotomy linked with the tail behaviour of the noise. When considering standard $α$-stable processes, very large jumps survive the interaction with the spatial complexity and yield anomalous, super-diffusive transport. In contrast, when the $α$-stable noise is either truncated or exponentially tempered, suppressing extremely long jumps, the transport undergoes a transition to a classical diffusive regime.
正文（点击展开）

正文（抓取，非 AI）

58. Native QR Factorization on Programmable Photonic Meshes

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.20701v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：We propose a photonic native procedure for computing the QR factorization of a matrix using a programmable unitary interferometer mesh. The method configures the mesh through a sequence of local power routing steps within tunable two mode interferometric elements, while reading out the resulting upper triangular factor directly from the optical outputs. The number of physical operations grows quadratically ($O(N^2)$) with matrix size, matching the information content of a dense input and reducing runtime relative to standard digital QR routines, which scale cubically ($O(N^3)$). Beyond single factorizations, the same architecture supports iterative spectral computations by reusing the configured interferometer in a mirrored arrangement that implements the core update step of the QR eigenvalue algorithm. We also describe related optical procedures for Hessenberg reduction and Bidiagonalization, serving as compatible preprocessors for QR and SVD workflows. Finally, we analyze the impact of finite control resolution on the computed factors.
正文（点击展开）

正文（抓取，非 AI）

59. The Universe Fan

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.21194v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：The wavefunction of the universe, as studied in perturbative quantum field theory, is a rational function whose singularities and factorization properties encode a rich underlying combinatorial structure. We define and study a broad generalization of such wavefunctions that can be associated to any lattice. We obtain these wavefunctions as the Laplace transform of a polyhedral fan, the universe fan, whose cones are defined by positivity conditions reflecting a notion of causality in the lattice, and we describe its face lattice. In the matroid case, the universe fan projects to the nested set fan, and the wavefunctions we define recover the matroid amplitudes introduced by Lam as residues. Moreover, in the case relevant for physics, the positivity conditions give a novel way to study the wavefunction, and we show how it is related to the cosmological polytopes of Arkani-Hamed, Benincasa, Postnikov. Finally, we study refinements of the universe fan induced by piecewise linear (tropical) functions. The resulting subdivisions project to refinements of the nested set fan and correspond dually to blow-ups of matroid polytopes, generalizing the cosmohedron polytope.
正文（点击展开）

正文（抓取，非 AI）

60. Delay Alignment Modulation for Secure ISAC Systems

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.21114v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：This paper introduces delay-alignment modulation (DAM) for secure integrated sensing and communication (ISAC). Due to the broadcast nature of multi-user downlinks, communications are vulnerable to eavesdropping. DAM applies controlled per-path symbol delays at the transmitter to coherently align the multipath components at the intended user, enhancing the received signal power, while simultaneously creating delay misalignment at the eavesdropper (Eve). To mitigate sensing degradation caused by multipath propagation, we propose a two-stage protocol that first estimates the angle and then the delay of the line-of-sight (LoS) path after suppressing multipath interference. We derive the secrecy spectral efficiency (SSE) and the Cramer-Rao (CRB) of the target delay. Finally, we develop a path-based zero-forcing (ZF) precoding framework and formulate a max-min SSE design under CRB and power constraints. Simulation results show DAM significantly outperforms the strongest-path (SP) benchmark in terms of SSE, while meeting sensing requirements, since intentional delay alignment at legitimate users degrades reception at Eve.
正文（点击展开）

正文（抓取，非 AI）

61. Entanglement-Induced Resilience of Quantum Dynamics

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.20987v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Quantum many-body devices suffer from imperfections that destabilize dynamics and limit scalability. We show that the dynamical growth of entanglement can intrinsically protect generic quantum dynamics against coherent and perturbative noise. Through rigorous theoretical analysis of general quantum dynamics and numerical simulations of spin chains and fermionic lattices, we prove that entanglement-entropy growth confines the influence of local Hamiltonian perturbations, thereby suppressing errors in dynamical errors. The degree of protection correlates quantitatively with the entanglement entropy of subsystems on which the perturbations act, and applies broadly to both analog quantum simulators and real-time control protocols. This entanglement-induced resilience is conceptually distinct from quantum error correction or dynamical decoupling: it passively leverages native many-body correlations without additional qubits, measurements, or control overhead. Our results reveal a generic mechanism linking entanglement growth to dynamical stability and provide practical guidelines for designing noise-resilient quantum devices.

62. Frontier Space-Time Algorithms Using Only Full Memory

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.21089v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：We develop catalytic algorithms for fundamental problems in algorithm design that run in polynomial time, use only $\mathcal{O}(\log(n))$ workspace, and use sublinear catalytic space matching the best-known space bounds of non-catalytic algorithms running in polynomial time. First, we design a polynomial time algorithm for directed $s$-$t$ connectivity using $n \big/ 2^{Θ(\sqrt{\log n})}$ catalytic space, which matches the state-of-the-art time-space bounds in the non-catalytic setting [Barnes et al., 1998], and improves the catalytic space usage of the best known algorithm [Cook and Pyne, 2026]. Furthermore, using only $\mathcal{O}(\log(n))$ random bits we get a randomized algorithm whose running time nearly matches the fastest time bounds known for space-unrestricted algorithms. Second, we design polynomial time algorithms for the problems of computing Edit Distance, Longest Common Subsequence, and the Discrete Fréchet Distance, again using $n \big/ 2^{Θ(\sqrt{\log n})}$ catalytic space. This again matches non-catalytic time-space frontier for Edit Distance and Least Common Subsequence [Kiyomi et al., 2021].

63. Training-Free Intelligibility-Guided Observation Addition for Noisy ASR

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.20967v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Automatic speech recognition (ASR) degrades severely in noisy environments. Although speech enhancement (SE) front-ends effectively suppress background noise, they often introduce artifacts that harm recognition. Observation addition (OA) addressed this issue by fusing noisy and SE enhanced speech, improving recognition without modifying the parameters of the SE or ASR models. This paper proposes an intelligibility-guided OA method, where fusion weights are derived from intelligibility estimates obtained directly from the backend ASR. Unlike prior OA methods based on trained neural predictors, the proposed method is training-free, reducing complexity and enhances generalization. Extensive experiments across diverse SE-ASR combinations and datasets demonstrate strong robustness and improvements over existing OA baselines. Additional analyses of intelligibility-guided switching-based alternatives and frame versus utterance-level OA further validate the proposed design.

64. Bikelution: Federated Gradient-Boosting for Scalable Shared Micro-Mobility Demand Forecasting

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.20671v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：The rapid growth of dockless bike-sharing systems has generated massive spatio-temporal datasets useful for fleet allocation, congestion reduction, and sustainable mobility. Bike demand, however, depends on several external factors, making traditional time-series models insufficient. Centralized Machine Learning (CML) yields high-accuracy forecasts but raises privacy and bandwidth issues when data are distributed across edge devices. To overcome these limitations, we propose Bikelution, an efficient Federated Learning (FL) solution based on gradient-boosted trees that preserves privacy while delivering accurate mid-term demand forecasts up to six hours ahead. Experiments on three real-world BSS datasets show that Bikelution is comparable to its CML-based variant and outperforms the current state-of-the-art. The results highlight the feasibility of privacy-aware demand forecasting and outline the trade-offs between FL and CML approaches.

65. Quantum Approximate Optimization for Decoding of Low-Density Parity-Check Codes

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.21124v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Decoding Low-Density Parity-Check (LDPC) codes is a fundamental problem in coding theory, and Belief Propagation (BP) is one of the most popular methods for LDPC code decoding. However, BP may encounter convergence issues and suboptimal performance, especially for short-length codes and in high-noise channels. The Quantum Approximate Optimization Algorithm (QAOA) is a type of Variational Quantum Algorithm (VQA) designed to solve combinatorial optimization problems by minimizing a problem-specific cost function. In this paper, we present a QAOA-based decoding framework for LDPC codes by formulating a decoding cost function that incorporates both parity-check constraints and soft channel reliability information. The resulting optimization problem is solved using QAOA to search for low-energy configurations corresponding to valid codewords. We test the proposed method through extensive numerical experiments and compare its performance with BP decoding. The experimental results demonstrate that the QAOA-based decoder achieves a higher probability of correctly recovering the transmitted codeword than BP across multiple experimental settings.

正文（抓取，非 AI）

66. TCDA: Robust 2D-DOA Estimation for Defective L-Shaped Arrays

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.21146v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：While tensor-based methods excel at Direction-of-Arrival (DOA) estimation, their performance degrades severely with faulty or sparse arrays that violate the required manifold structure. To address this challenge, we propose Tensor Completion for Defective Arrays (TCDA), a robust algorithm that reformulates the physical imperfection problem as a data recovery task within a virtual tensor space. We present a detailed derivation for constructing an incomplete third-order Parallel Factor Analysis (PARAFAC) tensor from the faulty array signals via subarray partitioning, cross-correlation, and dimensional reshaping. Leveraging the tensor's inherent low-rank structure, an Alternating Least Squares (ALS)-based algorithm directly recovers the factor matrices embedding the DOA parameters from the incomplete observations. This approach provides a software-defined 'self-healing' capability, demonstrating exceptional robustness against random element failures without requiring additional processing steps for DOA estimation.
正文（点击展开）

正文（抓取，非 AI）

67. A Micro-Macro Model of Encounter-Driven Information Diffusion in Robot Swarms

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.21148v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：In this paper, we propose the problem of Encounter-Driven Information Diffusion (EDID). In EDID, robots are allowed to exchange information only upon meeting. Crucially, EDID assumes that the robots are not allowed to schedule their meetings. As such, the robots have no means to anticipate when, where, and who they will meet. As a step towards the design of storage and routing algorithms for EDID, in this paper we propose a model of information diffusion that captures the essential dynamics of EDID. The model is derived from first principles and is composed of two levels: a micro model, based on a generalization of the concept of `mean free path'; and a macro model, which captures the global dynamics of information diffusion. We validate the model through extensive robot simulations, in which we consider swarm size, communication range, environment size, and different random motion regimes. We conclude the paper with a discussion of the implications of this model on the algorithms that best support information diffusion according to the parameters of interest.

68. Exact quantum transport in non-Markovian open Gaussian systems

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.21190v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：We build an exact framework to evaluate heat, energy, and particle transport between Gaussian reservoirs mediated by a quadratic quantum system. By combining full counting statistics with newly developed non-Markovian master equation approaches, we introduce an effective master equation whose solution can be used to generate arbitrary moments of the heat statistics for any number of reservoirs. This theory applies equally to fermionic and bosonic systems, holds at arbitrarily strong coupling, and resolves out-of-equilibrium transient dynamics determined by the system's initial state. In the steady-state, weak-coupling limit, we recover results analogous to those of the well-known Landauer-Büttiker formalism. We conclude our discussion by demonstrating an application of the method to a prototypical fermionic system. Our results uncover a regime of transient negative heat conductance contingent upon the initial system preparation, providing a clear signature of non-trivial out-of-equilibrium dynamics.
正文（点击展开）

正文（抓取，非 AI）

69. Optimal QAM Constellation for Over-the-Air Computation in the Presence of Heavy-Tailed Channel Noise

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.21027v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Over-the-air computation (OAC) enables low-latency aggregation over multiple-access channels (MACs) by exploiting the superposition property of the wireless medium to compute functions efficiently in distributed networks. A critical but often overlooked challenge is that electromagnetic interference in practical radio channels frequently exhibits heavy-tailed behavior, causing strong impulsive noise that severely degrades computation performance. This work studies digital OAC with QAM-based signaling under heavy-tailed interference modeled by a Cauchy distribution (lacking a finite second moment). We seek QAM-like constellations that minimize the mean-squared error (MSE) of sum aggregation subject to an average-power constraint. The problem is formulated as a constrained optimization, whose solution yields unique optimality conditions. Numerical results confirm the effectiveness of the proposed design. Notably, the framework extends naturally to nomographic functions, broader constellation families, and alternative noise models.
正文（点击展开）

正文（抓取，非 AI）

70. Squint: Fast Visual Reinforcement Learning for Sim-to-Real Robotics

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.21203v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Visual reinforcement learning is appealing for robotics but expensive -- off-policy methods are sample-efficient yet slow; on-policy methods parallelize well but waste samples. Recent work has shown that off-policy methods can train faster than on-policy methods in wall-clock time for state-based control. Extending this to vision remains challenging, where high-dimensional input images complicate training dynamics and introduce substantial storage and encoding overhead. To address these challenges, we introduce Squint, a visual Soft Actor Critic method that achieves faster wall-clock training than prior visual off-policy and on-policy methods. Squint achieves this via parallel simulation, a distributional critic, resolution squinting, layer normalization, a tuned update-to-data ratio, and an optimized implementation. We evaluate on the SO-101 Task Set, a new suite of eight manipulation tasks in ManiSkill3 with heavy domain randomization, and demonstrate sim-to-real transfer to a real SO-101 robot. We train policies for 15 minutes on a single RTX 3090 GPU, with most tasks converging in under 6 minutes.

正文（抓取，非 AI）

71. LST-SLAM: A Stereo Thermal SLAM System for Kilometer-Scale Dynamic Environments

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.20925v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Thermal cameras offer strong potential for robot perception under challenging illumination and weather conditions. However, thermal Simultaneous Localization and Mapping (SLAM) remains difficult due to unreliable feature extraction, unstable motion tracking, and inconsistent global pose and map construction, particularly in dynamic large-scale outdoor environments. To address these challenges, we propose LST-SLAM, a novel large-scale stereo thermal SLAM system that achieves robust performance in complex, dynamic scenes. Our approach combines self-supervised thermal feature learning, stereo dual-level motion tracking, and geometric pose optimization. We also introduce a semantic-geometric hybrid constraint that suppresses potentially dynamic features lacking strong inter-frame geometric consistency. Furthermore, we develop an online incremental bag-of-words model for loop closure detection, coupled with global pose optimization to mitigate accumulated drift. Extensive experiments on kilometer-scale dynamic thermal datasets show that LST-SLAM significantly outperforms recent representative SLAM systems, including AirSLAM and DROID-SLAM, in both robustness and accuracy.

72. SELAUR: Self Evolving LLM Agent via Uncertainty-aware Rewards

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.21158v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed as multi-step decision-making agents, where effective reward design is essential for guiding learning. Although recent work explores various forms of reward shaping and step-level credit assignment, a key signal remains largely overlooked: the intrinsic uncertainty of LLMs. Uncertainty reflects model confidence, reveals where exploration is needed, and offers valuable learning cues even in failed trajectories. We introduce SELAUR: Self Evolving LLM Agent via Uncertainty-aware Rewards, a reinforcement learning framework that incorporates uncertainty directly into the reward design. SELAUR integrates entropy-, least-confidence-, and margin-based metrics into a combined token-level uncertainty estimate, providing dense confidence-aligned supervision, and employs a failure-aware reward reshaping mechanism that injects these uncertainty signals into step- and trajectory-level rewards to improve exploration efficiency and learning stability. Experiments on two benchmarks, ALFWorld and WebShop, show that our method consistently improves success rates over strong baselines. Ablation studies further demonstrate how uncertainty signals e

  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models are advancing autonomous driving by replacing modular pipelines with unified end-to-end architectures. However, current VLAs face two expensive requirements: (1) massive dataset collection, and (2) dense reasoning annotations. In this work, we address both challenges with \modelname (\textbf{No} \textbf{R}easoning for \textbf{D}riving). Compared to existing VLAs, \modelname achieves competitive performance while being fine-tuned on $<$60\% of the data and no reasoning annotations, resulting in 3$\times$ fewer tokens. We identify that standard Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) fails to yield significant improvements when applied to policies trained on such small, reasoning-free datasets. We show that this limitation stems from difficulty bias, which disproportionately penalizes reward signals from scenarios that produce high-variance rollouts within GRPO. \modelname overcomes this by incorporating Dr.~GRPO, a recent algorithm designed to mitigate difficulty bias in LLMs. As a result, \modelname achieves competitive performance on Waymo and NAVSIM with a fraction of the training data and no reasoning overhead, enabling more efficient autono

74. On Hydrodynamic Formulations of Quantum Mechanics and the Problem of Sparse Ontology

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.21106v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Hydrodynamic reformulations of the Schrödinger equation suggest an interpretation of quantum mechanics in terms of a fluid flowing on configuration space. In the discrete hydrodynamic view, this fluid is not fundamental but emerges from many underlying microscopic fluid components whose collective behavior reproduces quantum phenomena. The most developed realization of this idea is the discrete many interacting worlds (MIW) framework, in which discrete particle-like worlds interact via inter-world forces and quantum probabilities are grounded in direct world counting. But there is also an older, continuous version of MIW. After reviewing the hydrodynamic and MIW formalisms, and emphasizing some of their interpretational advantages over the Everettian Many Worlds and Bohmian approaches, we argue that all discrete hydrodynamic models face a generic structural difficulty, which we call the problem of sparse ontology. Because wavefunctions typically branch under decoherence, the discrete components of the fluid are repeatedly partitioned into sub-ensembles, thereby thinning their density in configuration space and driving the dynamics away from the quantum regime once the components be

[2602.21106v1] On Hydrodynamic Formulations of Quantum Mechanics and the Problem of Sparse Ontology Quantum Physics arXiv:2602.21106v1 (quant-ph) [Submitted on 24 Feb 2026] Title: On Hydrodynamic Formulations of Quantum Mechanics and the Problem of Sparse Ontology Authors: Aric Hackebill , Bill Poirier View a PDF of the paper titled On Hydrodynamic Formulations of Quantum Mechanics and the Problem of Sparse Ontology, by Aric Hackebill and Bill Poirier View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: Hydrodynamic reformulations of the Schrödinger equation suggest an interpretation of quantum mechanics in terms of a fluid flowing on configuration space. In the discrete hydrodynamic view, this fluid is not fundamental but emerges from many underlying microscopic fluid components whose collective behavior reproduces quantum phenomena. The most developed realization of this idea is the discrete many interacting worlds (MIW) framework, in which discrete particle-like worlds interact via inter-world forces and quantum probabilities are grounded in direct world counting. But there is also an older, continuous version of MIW. After reviewing the hydrodynamic and MIW formalisms, and emphasizing some of their interpretational advantages over the Everettian Many Worlds and Bohmian approaches, we argue that all discrete hydrodynamic models face a generic structural difficulty, which we call the problem of sparse ontology. Because wavefunctions typically branch under decoherence, the discrete components of the fluid are repeatedly partitioned into sub-ensembles, thereby thinning their density in configuration space and driving the dynamics away from the quantum regime once the components become sufficiently sparse. We conclude that successful hydrodynamic completions of quantum mechanics plausibly require an essentially continuous ontology. 75. Detecting Where Effects Occur by Testing Hypotheses in Order

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.21068v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Experimental evaluations of public policies often randomize a new intervention within many sites or blocks. After a report of an overall result -- statistically significant or not -- the natural question from a policy maker is: \emph{where} did any effects occur? Standard adjustments for multiple testing provide little power to answer this question. In simulations modeled after a 44-block education trial, the Hommel adjustment -- among the most powerful procedures controlling the family-wise error rate (FWER) -- detects effects in only 11\% of truly non-null blocks. We develop a procedure that tests hypotheses top-down through a tree: test the overall null at the root, then groups of blocks, then individual blocks, stopping any branch where the null is not rejected. In the same 44-block design, this approach detects effects in 44\% of non-null blocks -- roughly four times the detection rate. A stopping rule and valid tests at each node suffice for weak FWER control. We show that the strong-sense FWER depends on how rejection probabilities accumulate along paths through the tree. This yields a diagnostic: when power decays fast enough relative to branching, no adjustment is needed;

[2602.21068v1] Detecting Where Effects Occur by Testing Hypotheses in Order Statistics > Methodology arXiv:2602.21068v1 (stat) [Submitted on 24 Feb 2026] Title: Detecting Where Effects Occur by Testing Hypotheses in Order Authors: Jake Bowers , David Kim , Nuole Chen View a PDF of the paper titled Detecting Where Effects Occur by Testing Hypotheses in Order, by Jake Bowers and 2 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: Experimental evaluations of public policies often randomize a new intervention within many sites or blocks. After a report of an overall result -- statistically significant or not -- the natural question from a policy maker is: \emph{where} did any effects occur? Standard adjustments for multiple testing provide little power to answer this question. In simulations modeled after a 44-block education trial, the Hommel adjustment -- among the most powerful procedures controlling the family-wise error rate (FWER) -- detects effects in only 11\% of truly non-null blocks. We develop a procedure that tests hypotheses top-down through a tree: test the overall null at the root, then groups of blocks, then individual blocks, stopping any branch where the null is not rejected. In the same 44-block design, this approach detects effects in 44\% of non-null blocks -- roughly four times the detection rate. A stopping rule and valid tests at each node suffice for weak FWER control. We show that the strong-sense FWER depends on how rejection probabilities accumulate along paths through the tree. This yields a diagnostic: when power decays fast enough relative to branching, no adjustment is needed; otherwise, an adaptive $\alpha$-adjustment restores control. We apply the method to 25 MDRC education trials and provide an R package, \texttt{manytestsr}. 76. Bypassing the Lyth Bound with Entangled Gravitons: Primordial Signatures and Late-Time Noise

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.20734v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：We demonstrate that quantum entanglement between primordial gravitons in dynamically decoupled gravitational sectors can parametrically enhance the tensor power spectrum during inflation. Unlike standard mechanisms relying on classical dynamics or modified actions, this enhancement originates from the reduced density matrix of the observable sector after tracing over a hidden gravitational reservoir. This framework allows for a sizable tensor-to-scalar ratio r > 0.01 consistent with sub-Planckian inflaton excursions, providing a purely quantum mechanical evasion of the Lyth bound. The resulting mixed state leaves a distinctive "quantum birthmark" in the form of oscillatory features in the power spectrum and a characteristic violation of the single-field consistency relation, manifesting as a scale-dependent enhancement of the squeezed-limit bispectrum. Furthermore, we forecast that this entanglement may manifest as a late-time stochastic noise enhancement in gravitational wave interferometers, offering a novel experimental window into the quantum nature of spacetime.

77. Reduced-order computational homogenization for hyperelastic media using gradient based sensitivity analysis of microstructures

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.20697v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：We propose an algorithm for the computational homogenization of locally periodic hyperelastic structures undergoing large deformations due to external quasi-static loading. The algorithm performs clustering of macroscopic deformations into subsets called "centroids", and, as a new ingredient, approximates the homogenized coefficients using sensitivity analysis of micro-configurations with respect to the macroscopic deformation. The novel "model-order reduction" approach significantly reduces the number of microscopic problems that must be solved in nonlinear simulations, thereby accelerating the overall computational process. The degree of reduction can be controlled by a user-defined error tolerance parameter. The algorithm is implemented in the finite element framework SfePy, and its performance effectiveness is demonstrated using two-dimensional test examples, when compared with solutions obtained by the proper orthogonal decomposition method, and by the full "FE-square" simulations. Extensions beyond the present implementations and the scope of tractable problems are discussed.

78. Airavat: An Agentic Framework for Internet Measurement

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.20924v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Internet measurement faces twin challenges: complex analyses require expert-level orchestration of tools, yet even syntactically correct implementations can have methodological flaws and can be difficult to verify. Democratizing measurement capabilities thus demands automating both workflow generation and verification against methodological standards established through decades of research. We present Airavat, the first agentic framework for Internet measurement workflow generation with systematic verification and validation. Airavat coordinates a set of agents mirroring expert reasoning: three agents handle problem decomposition, solution design, and code implementation, with assistance from a registry of existing tools. Two specialized engines ensure methodological correctness: a Verification Engine evaluates workflows against a knowledge graph encoding five decades of measurement research, while a Validation Engine identifies appropriate validation techniques grounded in established methodologies. Through four Internet measurement case studies, we demonstrate that Airavat (i) generates workflows matching expert-level solutions, (ii) makes sound architectural decisions, (iii) a

[2602.20924v1] Airavat: An Agentic Framework for Internet Measurement Computer Science > Networking and Internet Architecture arXiv:2602.20924v1 (cs) [Submitted on 24 Feb 2026] Title: Airavat: An Agentic Framework for Internet Measurement Authors: Alagappan Ramanathan , Eunju Kang , Dongsu Han , Sangeetha Abdu Jyothi View a PDF of the paper titled Airavat: An Agentic Framework for Internet Measurement, by Alagappan Ramanathan and 3 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: Internet measurement faces twin challenges: complex analyses require expert-level orchestration of tools, yet even syntactically correct implementations can have methodological flaws and can be difficult to verify. Democratizing measurement capabilities thus demands automating both workflow generation and verification against methodological standards established through decades of research. We present Airavat, the first agentic framework for Internet measurement workflow generation with systematic verification and validation. Airavat coordinates a set of agents mirroring expert reasoning: three agents handle problem decomposition, solution design, and code implementation, with assistance from a registry of existing tools. Two specialized engines ensure methodological correctness: a Verification Engine evaluates workflows against a knowledge graph encoding five decades of measurement research, while a Validation Engine identifies appropriate validation techniques grounded in established methodologies. Through four Internet measurement case studies, we demonstrate that Airavat (i) generates workflows matching expert-level solutions, (ii) makes sound architectural decisions, (iii) addresses novel problems without ground truth, and (iv) identifies methodological flaws missed by standard execution-based testing.   • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Physical-layer characteristics, such as channel state information (CSI) and transmitter noise induced by hardware impairments, are often uniquely associated with a transmitter. The proposed framework employs a partitioned equal-gain combining (P-EGC) scheme that leverages receiver diversity without requiring transmitter-specific CSI. 80. Is Multi-Distribution Learning as Easy as PAC Learning: Sharp Rates with Bounded Label Noise

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.21039v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Towards understanding the statistical complexity of learning from heterogeneous sources, we study the problem of multi-distribution learning. Given $k$ data sources, the goal is to output a classifier for each source by exploiting shared structure to reduce sample complexity. We focus on the bounded label noise setting to determine whether the fast $1/ε$ rates achievable in single-task learning extend to this regime with minimal dependence on $k$. Surprisingly, we show that this is not the case. We demonstrate that learning across $k$ distributions inherently incurs slow rates scaling with $k/ε^2$, even under constant noise levels, unless each distribution is learned separately. A key technical contribution is a structured hypothesis-testing framework that captures the statistical cost of certifying near-optimality under bounded noise-a cost we show is unavoidable in the multi-distribution setting. Finally, we prove that when competing with the stronger benchmark of each distribution's optimal Bayes error, the sample complexity incurs a \textit{multiplicative} penalty in $k$. This establishes a \textit{statistical} separation between random classification noise and Massart noise,

81. cyclinbayes: Bayesian Causal Discovery with Linear Non-Gaussian Directed Acyclic and Cyclic Graphical Models

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.21170v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：We introduce cyclinbayes, an open-source R package for discovering linear causal relationships with both acyclic and cyclic structures. The package employs scalable Bayesian approaches with spike-and-slab priors to learn directed acyclic graphs (DAGs) and directed cyclic graphs (DCGs) under non-Gaussian noise. A central feature of cyclinbayes is comprehensive uncertainty quantification, including posterior edge inclusion probabilities, posterior probabilities of network motifs, and posterior probabilities over entire graph structures. Our implementation addresses two limitations in existing software: (1) while methods for linear non-Gaussian DAG learning are available in R and Python, they generally lack proper uncertainty quantification, and (2) reliable implementations for linear non-Gaussian DCG remain scarce. The package implements computationally efficient hybrid MCMC algorithms that scale to large datasets. Beyond uncertainty quantification, we propose a new decision-theoretic approach to summarize posterior samples of graphs, yielding principled point estimates based on posterior expected loss such as posterior expected structural Hamming distance and structural intervention

82. Changing the Optics: Comparing Traditional and Retrieval-Augmented GenAI E-Tutorials in Interdisciplinary Learning

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.20544v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Understanding information-seeking behaviors in e-learning is critical, as learners must often make sense of complex and fragmented information, a challenge compounded in interdisciplinary fields with diverse prior knowledge. Compared to traditional e-tutorials, GenAI e-tutorials offer new ways to navigate information spaces, yet how they shape learners information-seeking behaviors remains unclear. To address this gap, we characterized behavioral differences between traditional and GenAI-mediated e-tutorial learning using the three search modes of orienteering. We conducted a between-subject study in which learners engaged with either a traditional e-tutorial or a GenAI e-tutorial accessing the same underlying information content. We found that the traditional users maintained greater awareness and focus of the information space, whereas GenAI users exhibited more proactive and exploratory behaviors with lower cognitive load due to the querying-driven interaction. These findings offer guidance for designing tutorials in e-learning.
正文（点击展开）

  • 摘要：Motivated by recent advances in digital quantum emulation using noisy intermediate-scale quantum (NISQ) devices and an increased interest in topological Green's function zeros in condensed matter systems, we here study Green's function zeros in topological Floquet systems. Just as in the case of continuum time evolution, topological bands of Green's function zeros may also contribute to the topological invariant. However, contrary to the case of continuum time evolution, Floquet Green's functions can have zeros even in the absence of interactions. 84. Automating Sensor Characterization with Bayesian Optimization

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.21661v2
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：The development of novel instrumentation requires an iterative cycle with three stages: design, prototyping, and testing. Recent advancements in simulation and nanofabrication techniques have significantly accelerated the design and prototyping phases. Nonetheless, detector characterization continues to be a major bottleneck in device development. During the testing phase, a significant time investment is required to characterize the device in different operating conditions and find optimal operating parameters. The total effort spent on characterization and parameter optimization can occupy a year or more of an expert's time. In this work, we present a novel technique for automated sensor characterization that aims to accelerate the testing stage of the development cycle. This technique leverages closed-loop Bayesian optimization (BO), using real-time measurements to guide parameter selection and identify optimal operating states. We demonstrate the method with a novel low-noise CCD, showing that the machine learning-driven tool can efficiently characterize and optimize operation of the sensor in a couple of days without supervision of a device expert.

[2509.21661v2] Automating Sensor Characterization with Bayesian Optimization Physics > Instrumentation and Detectors arXiv:2509.21661v2 (physics) [Submitted on 25 Sep 2025 ( v1 ), last revised 16 Jan 2026 (this version, v2)] Title: Automating Sensor Characterization with Bayesian Optimization Authors: J. Cuevas-Zepeda , C. Chavez , J. Estrada , J. Noonan , B. D. Nord , N. Saffold , M. Sofo-Haro , R. Spinola e Castro , S. Trivedi View a PDF of the paper titled Automating Sensor Characterization with Bayesian Optimization, by J. Cuevas-Zepeda and 8 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: The development of novel instrumentation requires an iterative cycle with three stages: design, prototyping, and testing. Recent advancements in simulation and nanofabrication techniques have significantly accelerated the design and prototyping phases. Nonetheless, detector characterization continues to be a major bottleneck in device development. During the testing phase, a significant time investment is required to characterize the device in different operating conditions and find optimal operating parameters. The total effort spent on characterization and parameter optimization can occupy a year or more of an expert's time. In this work, we present a novel technique for automated sensor characterization that aims to accelerate the testing stage of the development cycle. This technique leverages closed-loop Bayesian optimization (BO), using real-time measurements to guide parameter selection and identify optimal operating states. We demonstrate the method with a novel low-noise CCD, showing that the machine learning-driven tool can efficiently characterize and optimize operation of the sensor in a couple of days without supervision of a device expert. 85. Computing a Characteristic Orientation for Rotation-Independent Image Analysis

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.20930v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Handling geometric transformations, particularly rotations, remains a challenge in deep learning for computer vision. Standard neural networks lack inherent rotation invariance and typically rely on data augmentation or architectural modifications to improve robustness. Although effective, these approaches increase computational demands, require specialised implementations, or alter network structures, limiting their applicability. This paper introduces General Intensity Direction (GID), a preprocessing method that improves rotation robustness without modifying the network architecture. The method estimates a global orientation for each image and aligns it to a canonical reference frame, allowing standard models to process inputs more consistently across different rotations. Unlike moment-based approaches that extract invariant descriptors, this method directly transforms the image while preserving spatial structure, making it compatible with convolutional networks. Experimental evaluation on the rotated MNIST dataset shows that the proposed method achieves higher accuracy than state-of-the-art rotation-invariant architectures. [2602.20930v1] Computing a Characteristic Orientation for Rotation-Independent Image Analysis Computer Science > Computer Vision and Pattern Recognition arXiv:2602.20930v1 (cs) [Submitted on 24 Feb 2026] Title: Computing a Characteristic Orientation for Rotation-Independent Image Analysis Authors: Cristian Valero-Abundio , Emilio Sansano-Sansano , Raúl Montoliu , Marina Martínez García View a PDF of the paper titled Computing a Characteristic Orientation for Rotation-Independent Image Analysis, by Cristian Valero-Abundio and 3 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: Handling geometric transformations, particularly rotations, remains a challenge in deep learning for computer vision. Standard neural networks lack inherent rotation invariance and typically rely on data augmentation or architectural modifications to improve robustness. Although effective, these approaches increase computational demands, require specialised implementations, or alter network structures, limiting their applicability. This paper introduces General Intensity Direction (GID), a preprocessing method that improves rotation robustness without modifying the network architecture. The method estimates a global orientation for each image and aligns it to a canonical reference frame, allowing standard models to process inputs more consistently across different rotations. Unlike moment-based approaches that extract invariant descriptors, this method directly transforms the image while preserving spatial structure, making it compatible with convolutional networks. Experimental evaluation on the rotated MNIST dataset shows that the proposed method achieves higher accuracy than state-of-the-art rotation-invariant architectures. Additional experiments on the CIFAR-10 dataset, confirm that the method remains effective under more complex conditions.   • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.21151v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Understanding the locality of high-temperature plasma energy deposition on material surfaces in fusion reactors is critical for design. Here, we utilize the Gyrokinetic ElectroMagnetic turbulence including X-points (GEMX) simulation, together with SOLPS-ITER solutions for the background equilibrium electric field including drifts, to model the heat flux at the divertor plate and characterize the heat load width using realistic X-point geometry. We use a theory-based blobby transport model called the "Coherent Structure Transport" (CST) model to include the effect of plasma transport in the edge scrape-off layer. The CST model is extremely fast and can be used to quickly analyze any SOLPS-ITER solution. SOLPS-ITER provides the steady state, or equilibrium on which we superimpose blobby turbulence characterized by blob size, amplitude and frequency. We obtain the $1/B_p$ scaling of the heat load exponential decay width $λ_q$, in agreement with the Eich empirical scaling and with the Goldston heuristic theory. [2602.21151v1] A coherent structure transport model for scrape-off layer turbulence Physics > Plasma Physics arXiv:2602.21151v1 (physics) [Submitted on 24 Feb 2026] Title: A coherent structure transport model for scrape-off layer turbulence Authors: Zhichen Feng , James Myra , Junyi Cheng , Calder Haubrich , Yang Chen , Xinxing Ma , Darin R. Ernst , Scott Parker View a PDF of the paper titled A coherent structure transport model for scrape-off layer turbulence, by Zhichen Feng and 7 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: Understanding the locality of high-temperature plasma energy deposition on material surfaces in fusion reactors is critical for design. Here, we utilize the Gyrokinetic ElectroMagnetic turbulence including X-points (GEMX) simulation, together with SOLPS-ITER solutions for the background equilibrium electric field including drifts, to model the heat flux at the divertor plate and characterize the heat load width using realistic X-point geometry. We use a theory-based blobby transport model called the "Coherent Structure Transport" (CST) model to include the effect of plasma transport in the edge scrape-off layer. The CST model is extremely fast and can be used to quickly analyze any SOLPS-ITER solution. SOLPS-ITER provides the steady state, or equilibrium on which we superimpose blobby turbulence characterized by blob size, amplitude and frequency. We obtain the $1/B_p$ scaling of the heat load exponential decay width $\lambda_q$, in agreement with the Eich empirical scaling and with the Goldston heuristic theory. When including blobby turbulence in combination with the SOLPS-ITER electric field, we find a secondary peak in the heat flux radial profile, outwardly displaced from the strike point radius, with a relative amplitude that is proportional to the initial blob density. We describe the CST model in detail and provide initial investigations of the scaling of $\lambda_q$ and the secondary heat flux peak with blob size and amplitude. 87. A Granularity Characterization of Task Scheduling Effectiveness

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.20561v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Task-based runtime systems provide flexible load balancing and portability for parallel scientific applications, but their strong scaling is highly sensitive to task granularity. As parallelism increases, scheduling overhead may transition from negligible to dominant, leading to rapid drops in performance for some algorithms, while remaining negligible for others. Although such effects are widely observed empirically, there is a general lack of understanding how algorithmic structure impacts whether dynamic scheduling is always beneficial. In this work, we introduce a granularity characterization framework that directly links scheduling overhead growth to task-graph dependency topology. We show that dependency structure, rather than problem size alone, governs how overhead scales with parallelism. Based on this observation, we characterize execution behavior using a simple granularity measure that indicates when scheduling overhead can be amortized by parallel computation and when scheduling overhead dominates performance. [2602.20561v1] A Granularity Characterization of Task Scheduling Effectiveness Computer Science > Distributed, Parallel, and Cluster Computing arXiv:2602.20561v1 (cs) [Submitted on 24 Feb 2026] Title: A Granularity Characterization of Task Scheduling Effectiveness Authors: Sana Taghipour Anvar , David Kaeli View a PDF of the paper titled A Granularity Characterization of Task Scheduling Effectiveness, by Sana Taghipour Anvar and David Kaeli View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: Task-based runtime systems provide flexible load balancing and portability for parallel scientific applications, but their strong scaling is highly sensitive to task granularity. As parallelism increases, scheduling overhead may transition from negligible to dominant, leading to rapid drops in performance for some algorithms, while remaining negligible for others. Although such effects are widely observed empirically, there is a general lack of understanding how algorithmic structure impacts whether dynamic scheduling is always beneficial. In this work, we introduce a granularity characterization framework that directly links scheduling overhead growth to task-graph dependency topology. We show that dependency structure, rather than problem size alone, governs how overhead scales with parallelism. Based on this observation, we characterize execution behavior using a simple granularity measure that indicates when scheduling overhead can be amortized by parallel computation and when scheduling overhead dominates performance. Through experimental evaluation on representative parallel workloads with diverse dependency patterns, we demonstrate that the proposed characterization explains both gradual and abrupt strong-scaling breakdowns observed in practice. We further show that overhead models derived from dependency topology accurately predict strong-scaling limits and enable a practical runtime decision rule for selecting dynamic or static execution without requiring exhaustive strong-scaling studies or extensive offline tuning. 89. AIForge-Doc: A Benchmark for Detecting AI-Forged Tampering in Financial and Form Documents

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.20569v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：We present AIForge-Doc, the first dedicated benchmark targeting exclusively diffusion-model-based inpainting in financial and form documents with pixel-level annotation. Existing document forgery datasets rely on traditional digital editing tools (e.g., Adobe Photoshop, GIMP), creating a critical gap: state-of-the-art detectors are blind to the rapidly growing threat of AI-forged document fraud. AIForge-Doc addresses this gap by systematically forging numeric fields in real-world receipt and form images using two AI inpainting APIs -- Gemini 2.5 Flash Image and Ideogram v2 Edit -- yielding 4,061 forged images from four public document datasets (CORD, WildReceipt, SROIE, XFUND) across nine languages, annotated with pixel-precise tampered-region masks in DocTamper-compatible format.
